  550. February 1, 2014<br /><br />Although they advertise \\"Pack of 1200\\" there are definitely not more than 500. They came all mixed up in the 12 slot plastic organizer/storage disc, (i.e. finding stars in the place where there's mostly moons, and moons in teardrops and squares). I tried to shake it up and see if shipping caused the mixing of the different rhinestones, but they didn't mix up more; therefore they mixed up the shapes upon filling the disc at their factory. I have counted a few of the lesser filled slots, and all of the mostly filled up slots. Each slot has 20-30 rhinestones, placing the total rhinestones in this package to..... 240 to 360.<br /><br />I purchased this when it was 90% off, I would not purchased this if it had a higher price, and I do not suggest paying more than $2 for it. The \\"rhinestones\\" are of good quality, but clearly made out of plastic and not crystals or glass. (I expect rhinestones to be made out of crystals or glass, otherwise they should call them plastic gems.) The shapes that are the traditional gem shape, (i.e. square, rectangle, circle, teardrop) have nice cuts in them that make them sparkle and shine well in the light, but the other shapes (i.e. curved rain drop, moon, butterfly, flower) are not cut like a gem and do not sparkle, they just have the silver lining to shine. When one fell off my nail the silver backing still stuck to my nail.<br /><br />I doubt you could even fit 1200 pieces into this tiny disc. I'm glad I received something fun for my nails, but let this be a warning to others who might try to purchase this for their business/salon. There is under 400 \\"rhinestones\\" total, and there is not an evenly matched quantity across the 12 different shapes.<br /><br />Tweezers worked just fine to pick up and place them on my nails.<br /><br />Still waiting for this company's disc of \\"1200 pearls\\" to arrive, which I expect the same results from. Thanks for reading this far!<br /><br />April 12, 2014<br /><br />Still waiting...<br /><br />May 5, 2014<br /><br />Still waiting....<br /><br />May 7, 2014<br /><br />I ended up being tired of waiting, and submitted a claim to Amazon. I am not satisfied with this product at all by now. They promptly credited my account for the amount paid for the product. Thank you Amazon. Also, the pearl version mentioned earlier ended up being fine. I think this is a \\"hit or miss\\" company with their products.
